1. Express information. This includes things like saying what you see, what you know, and what you suspect.

2. Touch everything. This will help you understand the scene and any potential clues.

3. Think. This will help you come up with possible explanations for what you see.

4. Give clue. This can be anything from pointing out something obvious to giving you a lead on who to talk to.

5. Analyse. This will help you understand the crime and how it was committed. 
Therefore, among A through E, the answer is C.
